\Hypertarget{classpandas_1_1plotting_1_1__matplotlib_1_1core_1_1MPLPlot_a9f5949b034e12f03e3afa693923612ae}\index{pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot@{pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot}!\_apply\_axis\_properties@{\_apply\_axis\_properties}}
\index{\_apply\_axis\_properties@{\_apply\_axis\_properties}!pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot@{pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_apply\_axis\_properties()}{\_apply\_axis\_properties()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpandas_1_1plotting_1_1__matplotlib_1_1core_1_1MPLPlot_a9f5949b034e12f03e3afa693923612ae} 
 None pandas.\+plotting.\+\_\+matplotlib.\+core.\+MPLPlot.\+\_\+apply\+\_\+axis\+\_\+properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classmatplotlib_1_1axis_1_1Axis}{Axis}}}]{axis}{, }\item[{}]{rot}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{int \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} None }]{fontsize}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Tick creation within matplotlib is reasonably expensive and is
internally deferred until accessed as Ticks are created/destroyed
multiple times per draw. It's therefore beneficial for us to avoid
accessing unless we will act on the Tick.
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{classpandas_1_1plotting_1_1__matplotlib_1_1core_1_1MPLPlot_a37413e5c4598437277156e3c5839bf14}\index{pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot@{pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot}!\_parse\_errorbars@{\_parse\_errorbars}}
\index{\_parse\_errorbars@{\_parse\_errorbars}!pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot@{pandas.plotting.\_matplotlib.core.MPLPlot}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_parse\_errorbars()}{\_parse\_errorbars()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classpandas_1_1plotting_1_1__matplotlib_1_1core_1_1MPLPlot_a37413e5c4598437277156e3c5839bf14} 
 tuple\mbox{[}Any, \mbox{\hyperlink{classNDFrameT}{NDFrameT}}\mbox{]} pandas.\+plotting.\+\_\+matplotlib.\+core.\+MPLPlot.\+\_\+parse\+\_\+errorbars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{str}]{label}{, }\item[{}]{err}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classNDFrameT}{NDFrameT}}}]{data}{, }\item[{int     }]{nseries}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Look for error keyword arguments and return the actual errorbar data
or return the error DataFrame/dict

Error bars can be specified in several ways:
    Series: the user provides a pandas.Series object of the same
            length as the data
    ndarray: provides a np.ndarray of the same length as the data
    DataFrame/dict: error values are paired with keys matching the
            key in the plotted DataFrame
    str: the name of the column within the plotted DataFrame

Asymmetrical error bars are also supported, however raw error values
must be provided in this case. For a ``N`` length :class:`Series`, a
``2xN`` array should be provided indicating lower and upper (or left
and right) errors. For a ``MxN`` :class:`DataFrame`, asymmetrical errors
should be in a ``Mx2xN`` array.
\end{DoxyVerb}

 bool \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} list\mbox{[}tuple\mbox{[}int, ...\mbox{]}\mbox{]} pandas.\+plotting.\+\_\+matplotlib.\+core.\+MPLPlot.\+\_\+validate\+\_\+subplots\+\_\+kwarg (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} Sequence\mbox{[}Sequence\mbox{[}str\mbox{]}\mbox{]}}]{subplots}{, }\item[{Series \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} \mbox{\hyperlink{classpandas_1_1core_1_1frame_1_1DataFrame}{Data\+Frame}}}]{data}{, }\item[{str     }]{kind}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Validate the subplots parameter

- check type and content
- check for duplicate columns
- check for invalid column names
- convert column names into indices
- add missing columns in a group of their own
See comments in code below for more details.

Parameters
----------
subplots : subplots parameters as passed to PlotAccessor

Returns
-------
validated subplots : a bool or a list of tuples of column indices. Columns
in the same tuple will be grouped together in the resulting plot.
\end{DoxyVerb}
